If only </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:11">*globals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:12"> is provided, it must be a dictionary (and not a subclass of dictionary), which will be used for both the global and the local variables. If </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:13">*globals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:14"> and </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:15">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:16"> are given, they are used for the global and local variables, respectively. If provided, </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:17">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:18"> can be any mapping object. Remember that at module level, globals and locals are the same dictionary. If exec gets two separate objects as </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:19">*globals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:20"> and </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:21">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:22">, the code will be executed as if it were embedded in a class definition. If the </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:23">*globals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:24"> dictionary does not contain a value for the key </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:25">`__builtins__`</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:26">, a reference to the dictionary of the built-in module </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:27">`[builtins](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/builtins.html#module-builtins>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:28"> is inserted under that key. That way you can control what builtins are available to the executed code by inserting your own </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:29">`__builtins__`</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:30"> dictionary into </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:31">*globals*</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:32"> before passing it to </span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:33">`[exec()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bc455cbe9e0543458b62a0134e9ab983:34">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5e462835bf1f4dc4aa3225da9dab2348"><span data-offset-key="5e462835bf1f4dc4aa3225da9dab2348:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1dcce87aebc14b8f9b51fb11bcd3a176"><span data-offset-key="1dcce87aebc14b8f9b51fb11bcd3a176:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="8813815bb45a4fbba6bc981825946f9c"><span data-offset-key="8813815bb45a4fbba6bc981825946f9c:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="8813815bb45a4fbba6bc981825946f9c:1">`exec`</span><span data-offset-key="8813815bb45a4fbba6bc981825946f9c:2"> with the code object as the argument. Code compilation events may also be raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d"><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:0">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:1"> The built-in functions </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:2">`[globals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#globals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:3"> and </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:4">`[locals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:5"> return the current global and local dictionary, respectively, which may be useful to pass around for use as the second and third argument to </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:6">`[exec()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:7">. </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:8">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:9"> The default </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:10">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:11"> act as described for function </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:12">`[locals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:13"> below: modifications to the default </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:14">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:15"> dictionary should not be attempted. Pass an explicit </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:16">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:17"> dictionary if you need to see effects of the code on </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:18">*locals*</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:19"> after function </span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:20">`[exec()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#exec>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a09c106944d647b3ba9bb65c73161d3d:21"> returns.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc"><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:0">**`filter`**</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:2">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:4">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:5">)Construct an iterator from those elements of </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:6">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:7"> for which </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:8">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:9"> returns true. </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:10">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:11"> may be either a sequence, a container which supports iteration, or an iterator. If </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:12">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:13"> is </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:14">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:15">, the identity function is assumed, that is, all elements of </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:16">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:17"> that are false are removed. Note that </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:18">`filter(function, iterable)`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:19"> is equivalent to the generator expression </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:20">`(item for item in iterable if function(item))`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:21"> if function is not </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:22">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:23"> and </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:24">`(item for item in iterable if item)`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:25"> if function is </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:26">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:27">. See </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:28">`[itertools.filterfalse()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.filterfalse>)`</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:29"> for the complementary function that returns elements of </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:30">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:31"> for which </span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:32">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="14aa6f2e9b7845269047f19238b6abdc:33"> returns false.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7"><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:2">**`float`**</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:4">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:5">\])Return a floating point number constructed from a number or string </span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:6">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:7">. If the argument is a string, it should contain a decimal number, optionally preceded by a sign, and optionally embedded in whitespace. The optional sign may be </span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:8">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:9"> or </span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:10">`'-'`</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:11">; a </span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:12">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="d48963b8524f44b38fdab5a7850d9bf7:13"> sign has no effect on the value produced. The argument may also be a string representing a NaN (not-a-number), or a positive or negative infinity. More precisely, the input must conform to the following grammar after leading and trailing whitespace characters are removed:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630"><span data-offset-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630:1">`sign** ::= "+" | "-" **infinity** ::= "Infinity" | "inf" **nan** ::= "nan" **numeric_value** ::= [floatnumber](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#grammar-token-floatnumber>) | [infinity](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#grammar-token-infinity>) | [nan](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#grammar-token-nan>)**numeric_string** ::= [[sign](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#grammar-token-sign>)] [numeric_value](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#grammar-token-numeric-value>)`</span><span data-offset-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630:2"> Here </span><span data-offset-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630:3">`floatnumber`</span><span data-offset-key="38e20f1156a548228ad8e85c5d357630:4"> is the form of a Python floating-point literal, described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#floating" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e09a9e51963d4f90ae138945af7bc398"><span data-offset-key="e09a9e51963d4f90ae138945af7bc398:0">Floating point literals</span></span></a><span data-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5"><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:0">. Case is not significant, so, for example, ‚Äúinf‚Äù, ‚ÄúInf‚Äù, ‚ÄúINFINITY‚Äù and ‚ÄúiNfINity‚Äù are all acceptable spellings for positive infinity. Otherwise, if the argument is an integer or a floating point number, a floating point number with the same value (within Python‚Äôs floating point precision) is returned. If the argument is outside the range of a Python float, an </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:1">`[OverflowError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:2"> will be raised. For a general Python object </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:3">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:5">`float(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:6"> delegates to </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:7">`x.__float__()`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:8">. If </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:9">`__float__()`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:10"> is not defined then it falls back to </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:11">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:12">. If no argument is given, </span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:13">`0.0`</span><span data-offset-key="12dd412fa9b34994b793e01ea65807c5:14"> is returned. Examples:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b814ecdfc24046e1a270d605de89f772"><span data-offset-key="b814ecdfc24046e1a270d605de89f772:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="b814ecdfc24046e1a270d605de89f772:1">`>>>** float('+1.23') 1.23 **>>>** float(' -12345**\\n**') -12345.0 **>>>** float('1e-003') 0.001 **>>>** float('+1E6') 1000000.0 **>>>** float('-Infinity') -inf`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d19508dcbd6d4924ad1ecb2b4f08a53e"><span data-offset-key="d19508dcbd6d4924ad1ecb2b4f08a53e:0">The float type is described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="31898e19285d41598cb2dd99ec13d6c6"><span data-offset-key="31898e19285d41598cb2dd99ec13d6c6:0">Numeric Types ‚Äî int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef"><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:0">. </span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:1">*Changed in version 3.6:*</span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:2"> Grouping digits with underscores as in code literals is allowed. </span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:3">*Changed in version 3.7: x*</span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:4"> is now a positional-only parameter. </span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:5">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:6"> Falls back to </span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:7">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:8"> if </span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:9">`[__float__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__float__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="667e715607ae475d896133ce4000f1ef:10"> is not defined.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e"><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:0">**`format`**</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:2">*value*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:4">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:5">\])Convert a </span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:6">*value*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:7"> to a ‚Äúformatted‚Äù representation, as controlled by </span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:8">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:9">. The interpretation of </span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:10">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:11"> will depend on the type of the </span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:12">*value*</span><span data-offset-key="168526a01b3a4a4791d6a0482d75b45e:13"> argument, however there is a standard formatting syntax that is used by most built-in types: </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/string.html#formatspec" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0ef12266004141bbb9f0255edfe17564"><span data-offset-key="0ef12266004141bbb9f0255edfe17564:0">Format Specification Mini-Language</span></span></a><span data-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681"><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:0">. The default </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:1">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:2"> is an empty string which usually gives the same effect as calling </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:3">`[str(value)](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:4">. A call to </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:5">`format(value, format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:6"> is translated to </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:7">`type(value).__format__(value, format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:8"> which bypasses the instance dictionary when searching for the value‚Äôs </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:9">`[__format__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__format__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:10"> method. A </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:11">`[TypeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:12"> exception is raised if the method search reaches </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:13">`[object](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:14"> and the </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:15">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:16"> is non-empty, or if either the </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:17">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:18"> or the return value are not strings. </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:19">*Changed in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:20"> </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:21">`object().__format__(format_spec)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:22"> raises </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:23">`[TypeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:24"> if </span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:25">*format\_spec*</span><span data-offset-key="c7e0f87fea2a4bb29d629ec03e47d681:26"> is not an empty string.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d"><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:2">**`frozenset`**</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:4">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:5">\])Return a new </span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:6">`[frozenset](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset>)`</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:7"> object, optionally with elements taken from </span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:8">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:9">. </span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:10">`frozenset`</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:11"> is a built-in class. See </span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:12">`[frozenset](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#frozenset>)`</span><span data-offset-key="242a236d89be42ee8e5e24df9583df3d:13"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#types-set" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="767172caf4fb4985a8dfcef029810f21"><span data-offset-key="767172caf4fb4985a8dfcef029810f21:0">Set Types ‚Äî set, frozenset</span></span></a><span data-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c"><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:0"> for documentation about this class. For other containers see the built-in </span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:1">`[set](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#set>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:3">`[list](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:5">`[tuple](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#tuple>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:6">, and </span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:7">`[dict](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#dict>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:8"> classes, as well as the </span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:9">`[collections](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/collections.html#module-collections>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6eafc8bd872c4753b9342f29b429892c:10"> module.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84"><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:0">**`getattr`**</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:4">*name*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:6">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:7">\])Return the value of the named attribute of </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:8">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:9">. </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:10">*name*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:11"> must be a string. If the string is the name of one of the object‚Äôs attributes, the result is the value of that attribute. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:12">`getattr(x, 'foobar')`</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:13"> is equivalent to </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:14">`x.foobar`</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:15">. If the named attribute does not exist, </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:16">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:17"> is returned if provided, otherwise </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:18">`[AttributeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#AttributeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:19"> is raised. </span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:20">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="d447176ab7294971b61cece765978e84:21"> Since </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/expressions.html#private-name-mangling" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="2b6e6971f4b64641b4a5d29fd8bd4036"><span data-offset-key="2b6e6971f4b64641b4a5d29fd8bd4036:0">private name mangling</span></span></a><span data-key="df05f3e9100c47849ed6758dc9c54edc"><span data-offset-key="df05f3e9100c47849ed6758dc9c54edc:0"> happens at compilation time, one must manually mangle a private attribute‚Äôs (attributes with two leading underscores) name in order to retrieve it with </span><span data-offset-key="df05f3e9100c47849ed6758dc9c54edc:1">`[getattr()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#getattr>)`</span><span data-offset-key="df05f3e9100c47849ed6758dc9c54edc:2">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d48c97dd5bcf447e933f00e23b8e3927"><span data-offset-key="d48c97dd5bcf447e933f00e23b8e3927:0">**`globals`**</span><span data-offset-key="d48c97dd5bcf447e933f00e23b8e3927:1">()Return a dictionary representing the current global symbol table. This is always the dictionary of the current module (inside a function or method, this is the module where it is defined, not the module from which it is called).</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a"><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:0">**`hasattr`**</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:4">*name*</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:5">)The arguments are an object and a string. The result is </span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:6">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:7"> if the string is the name of one of the object‚Äôs attributes, </span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:8">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:9"> if not. (This is implemented by calling </span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:10">`getattr(object, name)`</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:11"> and seeing whether it raises an </span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:12">`[AttributeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#AttributeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="b7c34fa2777540ba840d58a5d586b65a:13"> or not.)</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90"><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:0">**`hash`**</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:3">)Return the hash value of the object (if it has one). Hash values are integers. They are used to quickly compare dictionary keys during a dictionary lookup. Numeric values that compare equal have the same hash value (even if they are of different types, as is the case for 1 and 1.0). </span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:4">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:5"> For objects with custom </span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:6">`[__hash__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:7"> methods, note that </span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:8">`[hash()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#hash>)`</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:9"> truncates the return value based on the bit width of the host machine. See </span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:10">`[__hash__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__hash__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="1b6dcded30cc4d83a4820f7d13d6cd90:11"> for details.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7"><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:0">**`help`**</span><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:1">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:3">\])Invoke the built-in help system. (This function is intended for interactive use.) If no argument is given, the interactive help system starts on the interpreter console. If the argument is a string, then the string is looked up as the name of a module, function, class, method, keyword, or documentation topic, and a help page is printed on the console. If the argument is any other kind of object, a help page on the object is generated. Note that if a slash(/) appears in the parameter list of a function, when invoking </span><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:4">`[help()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#help>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d5cdfa25c6754fac8353eeab988474e7:5">, it means that the parameters prior to the slash are positional-only. For more info, see </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/faq/programming.html#faq-positional-only-arguments" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="40cb04bceaf840c38ed446fb956136c0"><span data-offset-key="40cb04bceaf840c38ed446fb956136c0:0">the FAQ entry on positional-only parameters</span></span></a><span data-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86"><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:0">. This function is added to the built-in namespace by the </span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:1">`[site](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/site.html#module-site>)`</span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:2"> module. </span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:3">*Changed in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:4"> Changes to </span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:5">`[pydoc](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/pydoc.html#module-pydoc>)`</span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:6"> and </span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:7">`[inspect](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/inspect.html#module-inspect>)`</span><span data-offset-key="72e2b619bf7a4c5c843a0da4305c3b86:8"> mean that the reported signatures for callables are now more comprehensive and consistent.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69"><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:0">**`hex`**</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:2">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:3">)Convert an integer number to a lowercase hexadecimal string prefixed with ‚Äú0x‚Äù. If </span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:4">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:5"> is not a Python </span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:6">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:7"> object, it has to define an </span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:8">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="7f66c08de54a433880b3f5e5a887df69:9"> method that returns an integer. Some examples:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="487533fb977945d38f2caafbd521724b"><span data-offset-key="487533fb977945d38f2caafbd521724b:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="487533fb977945d38f2caafbd521724b:1">`>>>** hex(255) '0xff' **>>>** hex(-42) '-0x2a'`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ddf6667800814e5f851bc1d405509ab7"><span data-offset-key="ddf6667800814e5f851bc1d405509ab7:0">If you want to convert an integer number to an uppercase or lower hexadecimal string with prefix or not, you can use either of the following ways:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ff7d46e99c1c4ba3a11cd00c09f78154"><span data-offset-key="ff7d46e99c1c4ba3a11cd00c09f78154:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="ff7d46e99c1c4ba3a11cd00c09f78154:1">`>>>** '*%#x*' % 255, '*%x*' % 255, '*%X*' % 255 ('0xff', 'ff', 'FF') **>>>** format(255, '#x'), format(255, 'x'), format(255, 'X') ('0xff', 'ff', 'FF') **>>>** f'*{*255*:*#x*}*', f'*{*255*:*x*}*', f'*{*255*:*X*}*' ('0xff', 'ff', 'FF')`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f"><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:0">See also </span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:1">`[format()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#format>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:2"> for more information. See also </span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:3">`[int()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:4"> for converting a hexadecimal string to an integer using a base of 16. </span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:5">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:6"> To obtain a hexadecimal string representation for a float, use the </span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:7">`[float.hex()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#float.hex>)`</span><span data-offset-key="a76faeeaa92f4ef5a6135fc608d44e0f:8"> method.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855"><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:0">**`id`**</span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:3">)Return the ‚Äúidentity‚Äù of an object. This is an integer which is guaranteed to be unique and constant for this object during its lifetime. Two objects with non-overlapping lifetimes may have the same </span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:4">`[id()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#id>)`</span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:5"> value. </span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:6">**CPython implementation detail:**</span><span data-offset-key="e765cfa2d45d49a790721e4d29d15855:7"> This is the address of the object in memory. Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="35c56f3a8c3c47f191178ee956bee8b1"><span data-offset-key="35c56f3a8c3c47f191178ee956bee8b1:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9"><span data-offset-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9:1">`builtins.id`</span><span data-offset-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9:2"> with argument </span><span data-offset-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9:3">`id`</span><span data-offset-key="3f3e8e233b1e4149b485c376678696c9:4">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9"><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:0">**`input`**</span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:1">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:2">*prompt*</span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:3">\])If the </span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:4">*prompt*</span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:5"> argument is present, it is written to standard output without a trailing newline. The function then reads a line from input, converts it to a string (stripping a trailing newline), and returns that. When EOF is read, </span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:6">`[EOFError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#EOFError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="4fe24cc759c54a4cbb54f1b0218a97d9:7"> is raised. Example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="10dec578db304c44a5a5c92769968edd"><span data-offset-key="10dec578db304c44a5a5c92769968edd:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="10dec578db304c44a5a5c92769968edd:1">`>>>** s = input('--> ') --> Monty Python's Flying Circus **>>>** s "Monty Python's Flying Circus"`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941"><span data-offset-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941:0">If the </span><span data-offset-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941:1">`[readline](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/readline.html#module-readline>)`</span><span data-offset-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941:2"> module was loaded, then </span><span data-offset-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941:3">`[input()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#input>)`</span><span data-offset-key="e9fe661091584240aa1604e8509b2941:4"> will use it to provide elaborate line editing and history features.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c9bdacdc1d13476a87f6c90da0198130"><span data-offset-key="c9bdacdc1d13476a87f6c90da0198130:0">Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f5e8861115f14274a439e87bd3c7ed23"><span data-offset-key="f5e8861115f14274a439e87bd3c7ed23:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc"><span data-offset-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc:1">`builtins.input`</span><span data-offset-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc:2"> with argument </span><span data-offset-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc:3">`prompt`</span><span data-offset-key="cee347771d0d4ff5a2c1c6586aff8adc:4"> before reading input</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="818c57e442db48149620d3d72db8ebc6"><span data-offset-key="818c57e442db48149620d3d72db8ebc6:0">Raises an auditing event </span><span data-offset-key="818c57e442db48149620d3d72db8ebc6:1">`builtins.input/result`</span><span data-offset-key="818c57e442db48149620d3d72db8ebc6:2"> with the result after successfully reading input.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f"><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:2">**`int`**</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:4">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:5">\])</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:6">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:7"> </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:8">**`int`**</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:9">(</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:10">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:11">, </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:12">*base=10*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:13">)Return an integer object constructed from a number or string </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:14">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:15">, or return </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:16">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:17"> if no arguments are given. If </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:18">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:19"> defines </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:20">`[__int__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:21">, </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:22">`int(x)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:23"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:24">`x.__int__()`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:25">. If </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:26">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:27"> defines </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:28">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:29">, it returns </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:30">`x.__index__()`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:31">. If </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:32">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:33"> defines </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:34">`[__trunc__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__trunc__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:35">, it returns </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:36">`x.__trunc__()`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:37">. For floating point numbers, this truncates towards zero. If </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:38">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:39"> is not a number or if </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:40">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:41"> is given, then </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:42">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:43"> must be a string, </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:44">`[bytes](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:45">, or </span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:46">`[bytearray](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytearray>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c9b84a1ccf144fc99f3a2c8577f95e2f:47"> instance representing an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/reference/lexical_analysis.html#integers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="36f18003cafb4a23b40216afb5cb9f3b"><span data-offset-key="36f18003cafb4a23b40216afb5cb9f3b:0">integer literal</span></span></a><span data-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690"><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:0"> in radix </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:1">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:2">. Optionally, the literal can be preceded by </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:3">`+`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:4"> or </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:5">`-`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:6"> (with no space in between) and surrounded by whitespace. A base-n literal consists of the digits 0 to n-1, with </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:7">`a`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:8"> to </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:9">`z`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:10"> (or </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:11">`A`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:12"> to </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:13">`Z`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:14">) having values 10 to 35. The default </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:15">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:16"> is 10. The allowed values are 0 and 2‚Äì36. Base-2, -8, and -16 literals can be optionally prefixed with </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:17">`0b`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:18">/</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:19">`0B`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:20">, </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:21">`0o`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:22">/</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:23">`0O`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:24">, or </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:25">`0x`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:26">/</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:27">`0X`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:28">, as with integer literals in code. Base 0 means to interpret exactly as a code literal, so that the actual base is 2, 8, 10, or 16, and so that </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:29">`int('010', 0)`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:30"> is not legal, while </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:31">`int('010')`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:32"> is, as well as </span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:33">`int('010', 8)`</span><span data-offset-key="f191eb283ae24880b168b5e506ffe690:34">. The integer type is described in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesnumeric" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="4f607bff343c477ba1b75db83d6d256a"><span data-offset-key="4f607bff343c477ba1b75db83d6d256a:0">Numeric Types ‚Äî int, float, complex</span></span></a><span data-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9"><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:0">. </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:1">*Changed in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:2"> If </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:3">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:4"> is not an instance of </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:5">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:6"> and the </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:7">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:8"> object has a </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:9">`[base.__index__](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:10"> method, that method is called to obtain an integer for the base. Previous versions used </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:11">`[base.__int__](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:12"> instead of </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:13">`[base.__index__](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:14">. </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:15">*Changed in version 3.6:*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:16"> Grouping digits with underscores as in code literals is allowed. </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:17">*Changed in version 3.7: x*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:18"> is now a positional-only parameter. </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:19">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:20"> Falls back to </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:21">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:22"> if </span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:23">`[__int__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__int__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d87b7520bb8849328c21b23d67693fc9:24"> is not defined.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a"><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:0">**`isinstance`**</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:4">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:5">)Return </span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:6">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:7"> if the </span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:8">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:9"> argument is an instance of the </span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:10">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="c30a0e86755549e6b9b4c77fa24f153a:11"> argument, or of a (direct, indirect or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="bd72033db35c4a678528093938dce02c"><span data-offset-key="bd72033db35c4a678528093938dce02c:0">virtual</span></span></a><span data-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6"><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:0">) subclass thereof. If </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:1">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:2"> is not an object of the given type, the function always returns </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:4">. If </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:5">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:6"> is a tuple of type objects (or recursively, other such tuples), return </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:7">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:8"> if </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:9">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:10"> is an instance of any of the types. If </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:11">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:12"> is not a type or tuple of types and such tuples, a </span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:13">`[TypeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="1b4447683d7942469f5686e3a3da70d6:14"> exception is raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101"><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:0">**`issubclass`**</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:2">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:4">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:5">)Return </span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:6">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:7"> if </span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:8">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="af758d80d05e4a38bfc323ead443f101:9"> is a subclass (direct, indirect or </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-abstract-base-class" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ba49fce036b44b6b814bcf9f2f8d85b3"><span data-offset-key="ba49fce036b44b6b814bcf9f2f8d85b3:0">virtual</span></span></a><span data-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d"><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:0">) of </span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:1">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:2">. A class is considered a subclass of itself. </span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:3">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:4"> may be a tuple of class objects, in which case every entry in </span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:5">*classinfo*</span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:6"> will be checked. In any other case, a </span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:7">`[TypeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="31588da8da634b2cadef7d2180f8e51d:8"> exception is raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6"><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:0">**`iter`**</span><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:2">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:4">*sentinel*</span><span data-offset-key="ef6940cce480458c87f2dff2cfa722a6:5">\])Return an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="92644818bea8461985754e7226621cf7"><span data-offset-key="92644818bea8461985754e7226621cf7:0">iterator</span></span></a><span data-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b"><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:0"> object. The first argument is interpreted very differently depending on the presence of the second argument. Without a second argument, </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:1">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:2"> must be a collection object which supports the iteration protocol (the </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:3">`[__iter__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__iter__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:4"> method), or it must support the sequence protocol (the </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:5">`[__getitem__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__getitem__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:6"> method with integer arguments starting at </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:7">`0`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:8">). If it does not support either of those protocols, </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:9">`[TypeError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#TypeError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:10"> is raised. If the second argument, </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:11">*sentinel*</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:12">, is given, then </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:13">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:14"> must be a callable object. The iterator created in this case will call </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:15">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:16"> with no arguments for each call to its </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:17">`[__next__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:18"> method; if the value returned is equal to </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:19">*sentinel*</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:20">, </span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:21">`[StopIteration](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration>)`</span><span data-offset-key="9adf9af16d4d4a3eafd925cd95b8092b:22"> will be raised, otherwise the value will be returned. See also </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typeiter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c95da35dfa724ccbb0bc4cf6864c525c"><span data-offset-key="c95da35dfa724ccbb0bc4cf6864c525c:0">Iterator Types</span></span></a><span data-key="1e787dcc238743718742303a1f9a6e9a"><span data-offset-key="1e787dcc238743718742303a1f9a6e9a:0">. One useful application of the second form of </span><span data-offset-key="1e787dcc238743718742303a1f9a6e9a:1">`[iter()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#iter>)`</span><span data-offset-key="1e787dcc238743718742303a1f9a6e9a:2"> is to build a block-reader. For example, reading fixed-width blocks from a binary database file until the end of file is reached:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="f8281ae5b16b48d9aac967b3c5740469"><span data-offset-key="f8281ae5b16b48d9aac967b3c5740469:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="f8281ae5b16b48d9aac967b3c5740469:1">`from** **functools** **import** partial **with** open('mydata.db', 'rb') **as** f: **for** block **in** iter(partial(f.read, 64), b''): process_block(block)`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a"><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:0">**`len`**</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:2">*s*</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:3">)Return the length (the number of items) of an object. The argument may be a sequence (such as a string, bytes, tuple, list, or range) or a collection (such as a dictionary, set, or frozen set). </span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:4">**CPython implementation detail:**</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:5"> </span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:6">`len`</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:7"> raises </span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:8">`[OverflowError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OverflowError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:9"> on lengths larger than </span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:10">`[sys.maxsize](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.maxsize>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:11">, such as </span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:12">`[range(2 ** 100)](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#range>)`</span><span data-offset-key="d7250353a6d74a6e96ae18654bb8308a:13">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4"><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:2">**`list`**</span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:3">(\[</span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:4">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:5">\])Rather than being a function, </span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:6">`[list](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list>)`</span><span data-offset-key="54d14b03db804d16b632a1aebb76e5a4:7"> is actually a mutable sequence type, as documented in </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq-list" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="d31973dd6c314fb2aad103a42fa10d63"><span data-offset-key="d31973dd6c314fb2aad103a42fa10d63:0">Lists</span></span></a><span data-key="98ac222c2cc64a31b2c13cbe772c6d63"><span data-offset-key="98ac222c2cc64a31b2c13cbe772c6d63:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#typesseq" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1f2929731ea34989988337bd7f43410f"><span data-offset-key="1f2929731ea34989988337bd7f43410f:0">Sequence Types ‚Äî list, tuple, range</span></span></a><span data-key="a609dbd720c34dc8927616256790488e"><span data-offset-key="a609dbd720c34dc8927616256790488e:0">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f"><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:0">**`locals`**</span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:1">()Update and return a dictionary representing the current local symbol table. Free variables are returned by </span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:2">`[locals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:3"> when it is called in function blocks, but not in class blocks. Note that at the module level, </span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:4">`[locals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#locals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:5"> and </span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:6">`[globals()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#globals>)`</span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:7"> are the same dictionary. </span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:8">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="711e7e5a1952433ca1a93bca57ba326f:9"> The contents of this dictionary should not be modified; changes may not affect the values of local and free variables used by the interpreter.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf"><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:0">**`map`**</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:2">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:4">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:6">*...*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:7">)Return an iterator that applies </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:8">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:9"> to every item of </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:10">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:11">, yielding the results. If additional </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:12">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:13"> arguments are passed, </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:14">*function*</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:15"> must take that many arguments and is applied to the items from all iterables in parallel. With multiple iterables, the iterator stops when the shortest iterable is exhausted. For cases where the function inputs are already arranged into argument tuples, see </span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:16">`[itertools.starmap()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/itertools.html#itertools.starmap>)`</span><span data-offset-key="8aadff35cf3646a2812a848bf2f9bcbf:17">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796"><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:0">**`max`**</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:2">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:4">***\[, key***</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:5">**,**</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:6"> </span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:7">***default***</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:8">**\])**</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:9">`max`</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:10">\*(</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:11">*arg1*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:13">*arg2*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:14">, \*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:15">*args*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:16">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:17">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="6d7945bbf829422fb5fcd45cb0d3d796:18">\])Return the largest item in an iterable or the largest of two or more arguments. If one positional argument is provided, it should be an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="f5f3753c42844fef813091d109836e5f"><span data-offset-key="f5f3753c42844fef813091d109836e5f:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e"><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:0">. The largest item in the iterable is returned. If two or more positional arguments are provided, the largest of the positional arguments is returned. There are two optional keyword-only arguments. The </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:1">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:2"> argument specifies a one-argument ordering function like that used for </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:3">`[list.sort()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:4">. The </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:5">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:6"> argument specifies an object to return if the provided iterable is empty. If the iterable is empty and </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:7">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:8"> is not provided, a </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:9">`[ValueError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:10"> is raised. If multiple items are maximal, the function returns the first one encountered. This is consistent with other sort-stability preserving tools such as </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:11">`sorted(iterable, key=keyfunc, reverse=True)[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:12"> and </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:13">`heapq.nlargest(1, iterable, key=keyfunc)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:14">. </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:15">*New in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:16"> The </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:17">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:18"> keyword-only argument. </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:19">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:20"> The </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:21">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:22"> can be </span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:23">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="fd3df213da68412a8c21465bf386626e:24">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09"><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:2">**`memoryview`**</span><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:4">*object*</span><span data-offset-key="1adaea744c7f478aac90539c8065dd09:5">)Return a ‚Äúmemory view‚Äù object created from the given argument.
