<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171"><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:0">**`min`**</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:2">*iterable*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:4">***\[, key***</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:5">**,**</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:6"> </span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:7">***default***</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:8">**\])**</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:9">`min`</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:10">\*(</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:11">*arg1*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:12">, </span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:13">*arg2*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:14">, \*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:15">*args*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:16">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:17">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="5dd1b91722214571b3d3851f42a54171:18">\])Return the smallest item in an iterable or the smallest of two or more arguments. If one positional argument is provided, it should be an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-iterable" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3d12b6f0b21942b2ac55d312838d3432"><span data-offset-key="3d12b6f0b21942b2ac55d312838d3432:0">iterable</span></span></a><span data-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0"><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:0">. The smallest item in the iterable is returned. If two or more positional arguments are provided, the smallest of the positional arguments is returned. There are two optional keyword-only arguments. The </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:1">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:2"> argument specifies a one-argument ordering function like that used for </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:3">`[list.sort()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#list.sort>)`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:4">. The </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:5">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:6"> argument specifies an object to return if the provided iterable is empty. If the iterable is empty and </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:7">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:8"> is not provided, a </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:9">`[ValueError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:10"> is raised. If multiple items are minimal, the function returns the first one encountered. This is consistent with other sort-stability preserving tools such as </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:11">`sorted(iterable, key=keyfunc)[0]`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:12"> and </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:13">`heapq.nsmallest(1, iterable, key=keyfunc)`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:14">. </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:15">*New in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:16"> The </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:17">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:18"> keyword-only argument. </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:19">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:20"> The </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:21">*key*</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:22"> can be </span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:23">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="e2b2b3bbb7ec433ca11f3ce5a508d9e0:24">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86"><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:0">**`next`**</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:2">*iterator*</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:3">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:4">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:5">\])Retrieve the next item from the </span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:6">*iterator*</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:7"> by calling its </span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:8">`[__next__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#iterator.__next__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:9"> method. If </span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:10">*default*</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:11"> is given, it is returned if the iterator is exhausted, otherwise </span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:12">`[StopIteration](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#StopIteration>)`</span><span data-offset-key="ad344299ba4c4835966e49ec240d9a86:13"> is raised.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b"><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:1"> \*\*</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:2">`object`</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:3">\*\*Return a new featureless object. </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:4">`[object](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object>)`</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:5"> is a base for all classes. It has the methods that are common to all instances of Python classes. This function does not accept any arguments. </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:6">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:7"> </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:8">`[object](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object>)`</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:9"> does </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:10">*not*</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:11"> have a </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:12">`[__dict__](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#object.__dict__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:13">, so you can‚Äôt assign arbitrary attributes to an instance of the </span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:14">`[object](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#object>)`</span><span data-offset-key="10875855e64347dab8ce4efe3f1a6b5b:15"> class.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd"><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:0">**`oct`**</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:2">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:3">)Convert an integer number to an octal string prefixed with ‚Äú0o‚Äù. The result is a valid Python expression. If </span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:4">*x*</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:5"> is not a Python </span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:6">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:7"> object, it has to define an </span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:8">`[__index__()](<https://docs.python.org/3/reference/datamodel.html#object.__index__>)`</span><span data-offset-key="6aa78ffc26cb4baea0b6d52ed10013bd:9"> method that returns an integer. For example:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="1c3617420b224c668db8b4557f0202a1"><span data-offset-key="1c3617420b224c668db8b4557f0202a1:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="1c3617420b224c668db8b4557f0202a1:1">`>>>** oct(8) '0o10' **>>>** oct(-56) '-0o70'`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="989fec9e51164627aaed74f8e345b74c"><span data-offset-key="989fec9e51164627aaed74f8e345b74c:0">If you want to convert an integer number to octal string either with prefix ‚Äú0o‚Äù or not, you can use either of the following ways.&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="9494403af062420b9f844ce998659baf"><span data-offset-key="9494403af062420b9f844ce998659baf:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="9494403af062420b9f844ce998659baf:1">`>>>** '*%#o*' % 10, '*%o*' % 10 ('0o12', '12') **>>>** format(10, '#o'), format(10, 'o') ('0o12', '12') **>>>** f'*{*10*:*#o*}*', f'*{*10*:*o*}*' ('0o12', '12')`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ec4be3221b974134a04bc3da7c14b0fd"><span data-offset-key="ec4be3221b974134a04bc3da7c14b0fd:0">See also </span><span data-offset-key="ec4be3221b974134a04bc3da7c14b0fd:1">`[format()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#format>)`</span><span data-offset-key="ec4be3221b974134a04bc3da7c14b0fd:2"> for more information.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0"><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:0">**`open`**</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:2">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:4">*mode='r'*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:6">*buffering=-1*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:8">*encoding=None*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:10">*errors=None*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:11">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:12">*newline=None*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:13">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:14">*closefd=True*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:15">, </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:16">*opener=None*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:17">)Open </span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:18">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="bc45b269929e4c03a3123aa0e76f30b0:19"> and return a corresponding </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="c892750af635470dbf05deff61d8cadd"><span data-offset-key="c892750af635470dbf05deff61d8cadd:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="7b708eded8284e41af39798d64903a6a"><span data-offset-key="7b708eded8284e41af39798d64903a6a:0">. If the file cannot be opened, an </span><span data-offset-key="7b708eded8284e41af39798d64903a6a:1">`[OSError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OSError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="7b708eded8284e41af39798d64903a6a:2"> is raised. See </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/tutorial/inputoutput.html#tut-files" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="687c671c054f47d480e4911e15c01840"><span data-offset-key="687c671c054f47d480e4911e15c01840:0">Reading and Writing Files</span></span></a><span data-key="228dab0ebffe4c6cb2249d6561c089dc"><span data-offset-key="228dab0ebffe4c6cb2249d6561c089dc:0"> for more examples of how to use this function. </span><span data-offset-key="228dab0ebffe4c6cb2249d6561c089dc:1">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="228dab0ebffe4c6cb2249d6561c089dc:2"> is a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-path-like-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8efcd2fd235a4fafab94863445d5bd17"><span data-offset-key="8efcd2fd235a4fafab94863445d5bd17:0">path-like object</span></span></a><span data-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035"><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:0"> giving the pathname (absolute or relative to the current working directory) of the file to be opened or an integer file descriptor of the file to be wrapped. (If a file descriptor is given, it is closed when the returned I/O object is closed, unless </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:1">*closefd*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:2"> is set to </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:3">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:4">.) </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:5">*mode*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:6"> is an optional string that specifies the mode in which the file is opened. It defaults to </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:7">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:8"> which means open for reading in text mode. Other common values are </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:9">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:10"> for writing (truncating the file if it already exists), </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:11">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:12"> for exclusive creation and </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:13">`'a'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:14"> for appending (which on </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:15">*some*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:16"> Unix systems, means that </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:17">*all*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:18"> writes append to the end of the file regardless of the current seek position). In text mode, if </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:19">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:20"> is not specified the encoding used is platform dependent: </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:21">`locale.getpreferredencoding(False)`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:22"> is called to get the current locale encoding. (For reading and writing raw bytes use binary mode and leave </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:23">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:24"> unspecified.) The available modes are:CharacterMeaning</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:25">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:26">open for reading (default)</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:27">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:28">open for writing, truncating the file first</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:29">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:30">open for exclusive creation, failing if the file already exists</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:31">`'a'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:32">open for writing, appending to the end of the file if it exists</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:33">`'b'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:34">binary mode</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:35">`'t'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:36">text mode (default)</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:37">`'+'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:38">open for updating (reading and writing) The default mode is </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:39">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:40"> (open for reading text, synonym of </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:41">`'rt'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:42">). Modes </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:43">`'w+'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:44"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:45">`'w+b'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:46"> open and truncate the file. Modes </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:47">`'r+'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:48"> and </span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:49">`'r+b'`</span><span data-offset-key="ae86c90503624c799cc85ca484817035:50"> open the file with no truncation. As mentioned in the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io-overview" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ec5b8a6d1abe49e797cf3f2c431c7390"><span data-offset-key="ec5b8a6d1abe49e797cf3f2c431c7390:0">Overview</span></span></a><span data-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53"><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:0">, Python distinguishes between binary and text I/O. Files opened in binary mode (including </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:1">`'b'`</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:2"> in the </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:3">*mode*</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:4"> argument) return contents as </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:5">`[bytes](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#bytes>)`</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:6"> objects without any decoding. In text mode (the default, or when </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:7">`'t'`</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:8"> is included in the </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:9">*mode*</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:10"> argument), the contents of the file are returned as </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:11">`[str](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str>)`</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:12">, the bytes having been first decoded using a platform-dependent encoding or using the specified </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:13">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:14"> if given. There is an additional mode character permitted, </span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:15">`'U'`</span><span data-offset-key="8484bfc283594b3f82c68ba2590b3e53:16">, which no longer has any effect, and is considered deprecated. It previously enabled </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="fa3c0c912de845998f6d4c4e9d88770e"><span data-offset-key="fa3c0c912de845998f6d4c4e9d88770e:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="9919606827064d8e9c29d4c4cc3fe358"><span data-offset-key="9919606827064d8e9c29d4c4cc3fe358:0"> in text mode, which became the default behaviour in Python 3.0. Refer to the documentation of the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open-newline-parameter" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="195ee6619de94695a9be7e850ff21c2d"><span data-offset-key="195ee6619de94695a9be7e850ff21c2d:0">newline</span></span></a><span data-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03"><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:0"> parameter for further details. </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:1">**Note**</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:2"> Python doesn‚Äôt depend on the underlying operating system‚Äôs notion of text files; all the processing is done by Python itself, and is therefore platform-independent. </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:3">*buffering*</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:4"> is an optional integer used to set the buffering policy. Pass 0 to switch buffering off (only allowed in binary mode), 1 to select line buffering (only usable in text mode), and an integer &gt; 1 to indicate the size in bytes of a fixed-size chunk buffer. When no </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:5">*buffering*</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:6"> argument is given, the default buffering policy works as follows: ‚Ä¢ Binary files are buffered in fixed-size chunks; the size of the buffer is chosen using a heuristic trying to determine the underlying device‚Äôs ‚Äúblock size‚Äù and falling back on </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:7">`[io.DEFAULT_BUFFER_SIZE](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.DEFAULT_BUFFER_SIZE>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:8">. On many systems, the buffer will typically be 4096 or 8192 bytes long. ‚Ä¢ ‚ÄúInteractive‚Äù text files (files for which </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:9">`[isatty()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.IOBase.isatty>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:10"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:11">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:12">) use line buffering. Other text files use the policy described above for binary files. </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:13">*encoding*</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:14"> is the name of the encoding used to decode or encode the file. This should only be used in text mode. The default encoding is platform dependent (whatever </span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:15">`[locale.getpreferredencoding()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/locale.html#locale.getpreferredencoding>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fe52198123f949cea7f6a6d699ef7b03:16"> returns), but any </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-text-encoding" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="75ab8c1953f749789eeeef0234c638ee"><span data-offset-key="75ab8c1953f749789eeeef0234c638ee:0">text encoding</span></span></a><span data-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765"><span data-offset-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765:0"> supported by Python can be used. See the </span><span data-offset-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765:1">`[codecs](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#module-codecs>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765:2"> module for the list of supported encodings. </span><span data-offset-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765:3">*errors*</span><span data-offset-key="c896a1f0cb384cef8ab1e727fbdf8765:4"> is an optional string that specifies how encoding and decoding errors are to be handled‚Äîthis cannot be used in binary mode. A variety of standard error handlers are available (listed under </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#error-handlers" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="68e8b4896f624736960e677a1ea60737"><span data-offset-key="68e8b4896f624736960e677a1ea60737:0">Error Handlers</span></span></a><span data-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5"><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:0">), though any error handling name that has been registered with </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:1">`[codecs.register_error()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/codecs.html#codecs.register_error>)`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:2"> is also valid. The standard names include: ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:3">`'strict'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:4"> to raise a </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:5">`[ValueError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#ValueError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:6"> exception if there is an encoding error. The default value of </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:7">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:8"> has the same effect. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:9">`'ignore'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:10"> ignores errors. Note that ignoring encoding errors can lead to data loss. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:11">`'replace'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:12"> causes a replacement marker (such as </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:13">`'?'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:14">) to be inserted where there is malformed data. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:15">`'surrogateescape'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:16"> will represent any incorrect bytes as code points in the Unicode Private Use Area ranging from U+DC80 to U+DCFF. These private code points will then be turned back into the same bytes when the </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:17">`surrogateescape`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:18"> error handler is used when writing data. This is useful for processing files in an unknown encoding. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:19">`'xmlcharrefreplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:20"> is only supported when writing to a file. Characters not supported by the encoding are replaced with the appropriate XML character reference </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:21">`&#nnn;`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:22">. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:23">`'backslashreplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:24"> replaces malformed data by Python‚Äôs backslashed escape sequences. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:25">`'namereplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:26"> (also only supported when writing) replaces unsupported characters with </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:27">`\\N{...}`</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:28"> escape sequences. </span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:29">*newline*</span><span data-offset-key="cd313b1cd22b4e8c8774eb28ef29a6e5:30"> controls how </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-universal-newlines" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="ad2e3a16eb9d4c448a1c85bcf97d7863"><span data-offset-key="ad2e3a16eb9d4c448a1c85bcf97d7863:0">universal newlines</span></span></a><span data-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c"><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:0"> mode works (it only applies to text mode). It can be </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:1">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:2">, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:3">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:5">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:7">`'\\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:8">, and </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:9">`'\\r\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:10">. It works as follows: ‚Ä¢ When reading input from the stream, if </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:11">*newline*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:12"> is </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:13">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:14">, universal newlines mode is enabled. Lines in the input can end in </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:15">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:16">, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:17">`'\\r'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:18">, or </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:19">`'\\r\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:20">, and these are translated into </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:21">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:22"> before being returned to the caller. If it is </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:23">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:24">, universal newlines mode is enabled, but line endings are returned to the caller untranslated. If it has any of the other legal values, input lines are only terminated by the given string, and the line ending is returned to the caller untranslated. ‚Ä¢ When writing output to the stream, if </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:25">*newline*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:26"> is </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:27">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:28">, any </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:29">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:30"> characters written are translated to the system default line separator, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:31">`[os.linesep](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.linesep>)`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:32">. If </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:33">*newline*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:34"> is </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:35">`''`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:36"> or </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:37">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:38">, no translation takes place. If </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:39">*newline*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:40"> is any of the other legal values, any </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:41">`'\\n'`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:42"> characters written are translated to the given string. If </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:43">*closefd*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:44"> is </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:45">`False`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:46"> and a file descriptor rather than a filename was given, the underlying file descriptor will be kept open when the file is closed. If a filename is given </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:47">*closefd*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:48"> must be </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:49">`True`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:50"> (the default) otherwise an error will be raised. A custom opener can be used by passing a callable as </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:51">*opener*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:52">. The underlying file descriptor for the file object is then obtained by calling </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:53">*opener*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:54"> with (</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:55">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:56">, </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:57">*flags*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:58">). </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:59">*opener*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:60"> must return an open file descriptor (passing </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:61">`[os.open](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.open>)`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:62"> as </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:63">*opener*</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:64"> results in functionality similar to passing </span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:65">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="b88b81320ec24838b9e37d9746e4dc4c:66">). The newly created file is </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#fd-inheritance" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="b5018e3a5f784d42b368d58da2a280b6"><span data-offset-key="b5018e3a5f784d42b368d58da2a280b6:0">non-inheritable</span></span></a><span data-key="6d36ee48df624de2ad3b28f5074e77f4"><span data-offset-key="6d36ee48df624de2ad3b28f5074e77f4:0">. The following example uses the </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#dir-fd" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="e18abcb3fc8d44d6bdc9afea3acddee6"><span data-offset-key="e18abcb3fc8d44d6bdc9afea3acddee6:0">dir_fd</span></span></a><span data-key="531e6886c9f2464fa993e401b3ca3b3e"><span data-offset-key="531e6886c9f2464fa993e401b3ca3b3e:0"> parameter of the </span><span data-offset-key="531e6886c9f2464fa993e401b3ca3b3e:1">`[os.open()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.open>)`</span><span data-offset-key="531e6886c9f2464fa993e401b3ca3b3e:2"> function to open a file relative to a given directory:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c255f318edf540c792bb4fced05a42c2"><span data-offset-key="c255f318edf540c792bb4fced05a42c2:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="c255f318edf540c792bb4fced05a42c2:1">`>>> import** **os>>>** dir_fd = os.open('somedir', os.O_RDONLY) **>>> def** opener(path, flags): **...** **return** os.open(path, flags, dir_fd=dir_fd) **...>>> with** open('spamspam.txt', 'w', opener=opener) **as** f: **...** print('This will be written to somedir/spamspam.txt', file=f) **...>>>** os.close(dir_fd) *# don't leak a file descriptor*`</span><span data-offset-key="c255f318edf540c792bb4fced05a42c2:2"> The type of </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-file-object" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="3dfeaf510f394abab0edbc806d2a9b04"><span data-offset-key="3dfeaf510f394abab0edbc806d2a9b04:0">file object</span></span></a><span data-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730"><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:0"> returned by the </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:1">`[open()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:2"> function depends on the mode. When </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:3">`[open()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:4"> is used to open a file in a text mode (</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:5">`'w'`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:7">`'r'`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:9">`'wt'`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:10">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:11">`'rt'`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:12">, etc.), it returns a subclass of </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:13">`[io.TextIOBase](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.TextIOBase>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:14"> (specifically </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:15">`[io.TextIOWrapper](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.TextIOWrapper>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:16">). When used to open a file in a binary mode with buffering, the returned class is a subclass of </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:17">`[io.BufferedIOBase](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedIOBase>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:18">. The exact class varies: in read binary mode, it returns an </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:19">`[io.BufferedReader](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedReader>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:20">; in write binary and append binary modes, it returns an </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:21">`[io.BufferedWriter](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedWriter>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:22">, and in read/write mode, it returns an </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:23">`[io.BufferedRandom](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.BufferedRandom>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:24">. When buffering is disabled, the raw stream, a subclass of </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:25">`[io.RawIOBase](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.RawIOBase>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:26">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:27">`[io.FileIO](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.FileIO>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:28">, is returned. See also the file handling modules, such as, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:29">`[fileinput](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/fileinput.html#module-fileinput>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:30">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:31">`[io](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#module-io>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:32"> (where </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:33">`[open()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#open>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:34"> is declared), </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:35">`[os](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#module-os>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:36">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:37">`[os.path](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.path.html#module-os.path>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:38">, </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:39">`[tempfile](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/tempfile.html#module-tempfile>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:40">, and </span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:41">`[shutil](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/shutil.html#module-shutil>)`</span><span data-offset-key="bd41bb81e9ae4690bcfb6a22bc9f0730:42">. Raises an </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#auditing" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0cc79d858b5e41c4a008269a4cdb2c57"><span data-offset-key="0cc79d858b5e41c4a008269a4cdb2c57:0">auditing event</span></span></a><span data-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf"><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:0"> </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:1">`open`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:2"> with arguments </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:3">`file`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:5">`mode`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:6">, </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:7">`flags`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:8">. The </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:9">`mode`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:10"> and </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:11">`flags`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:12"> arguments may have been modified or inferred from the original call.</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:13">*Changed in version 3.3:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:14"> ‚Ä¢ The </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:15">*opener*</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:16"> parameter was added. ‚Ä¢ The </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:17">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:18"> mode was added. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:19">`[IOError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#IOError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:20"> used to be raised, it is now an alias of </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:21">`[OSError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#OSError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:22">. ‚Ä¢ </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:23">`[FileExistsError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#FileExistsError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:24"> is now raised if the file opened in exclusive creation mode (</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:25">`'x'`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:26">) already exists.</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:27">*Changed in version 3.4:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:28"> ‚Ä¢ The file is now non-inheritable. </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:29">*Deprecated since version 3.4, will be removed in version 3.10:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:30"> The </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:31">`'U'`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:32"> mode.</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:33">*Changed in version 3.5:*</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:34"> ‚Ä¢ If the system call is interrupted and the signal handler does not raise an exception, the function now retries the system call instead of raising an </span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:35">`[InterruptedError](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/exceptions.html#InterruptedError>)`</span><span data-offset-key="fd6a6b3f24044c32908939c87d668dcf:36"> exception (see </span></span><a href="https://www.python.org/dev/peps/pep-0475" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="0bc8e71d7876403e8d2d63e6c5eaad9b"><span data-offset-key="0bc8e71d7876403e8d2d63e6c5eaad9b:0"><strong>PEP 475</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196"><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:0"> for the rationale). ‚Ä¢ The </span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:1">`'namereplace'`</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:2"> error handler was added.</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:3">*Changed in version 3.6:*</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:4"> ‚Ä¢ Support added to accept objects implementing </span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:5">`[os.PathLike](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/os.html#os.PathLike>)`</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:6">. ‚Ä¢ On Windows, opening a console buffer may return a subclass of </span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:7">`[io.RawIOBase](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.RawIOBase>)`</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:8"> other than </span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:9">`[io.FileIO](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/io.html#io.FileIO>)`</span><span data-offset-key="346e1827d5ff408798119f36499df196:10">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854"><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:0">**`ord`**</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:2">*c*</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:3">)Given a string representing one Unicode character, return an integer representing the Unicode code point of that character. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:4">`ord('a')`</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:5"> returns the integer </span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:6">`97`</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:7"> and </span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:8">`ord('‚Ç¨')`</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:9"> (Euro sign) returns </span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:10">`8364`</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:11">. This is the inverse of </span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:12">`[chr()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#chr>)`</span><span data-offset-key="892fe8e121d14f85b280fd4185898854:13">.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9"><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:0">**`pow`**</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:1">(</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:2">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:4">*exp*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:5">\[, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:6">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:7">\])Return </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:8">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:9"> to the power </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:10">*exp*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:11">; if </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:12">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:13"> is present, return </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:14">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:15"> to the power </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:16">*exp*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:17">, modulo </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:18">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:19"> (computed more efficiently than </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:20">`pow(base, exp) % mod`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:21">). The two-argument form </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:22">`pow(base, exp)`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:23"> is equivalent to using the power operator: </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:24">`base**exp`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:25">. The arguments must have numeric types. With mixed operand types, the coercion rules for binary arithmetic operators apply. For </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:26">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:27"> operands, the result has the same type as the operands (after coercion) unless the second argument is negative; in that case, all arguments are converted to float and a float result is delivered. For example, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:28">`10**2`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:29"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:30">`100`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:31">, but </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:32">`10**-2`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:33"> returns </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:34">`0.01`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:35">. For </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:36">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:37"> operands </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:38">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:39"> and </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:40">*exp*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:41">, if </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:42">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:43"> is present, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:44">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:45"> must also be of integer type and </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:46">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:47"> must be nonzero. If </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:48">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:49"> is present and </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:50">*exp*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:51"> is negative, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:52">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:53"> must be relatively prime to </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:54">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:55">. In that case, </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:56">`pow(inv_base, -exp, mod)`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:57"> is returned, where </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:58">*inv\_base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:59"> is an inverse to </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:60">*base*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:61"> modulo </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:62">*mod*</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:63">. Here‚Äôs an example of computing an inverse for </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:64">`38`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:65"> modulo </span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:66">`97`</span><span data-offset-key="c62ee34ffb6a48bdab76ce626598a5b9:67">:&gt;&gt;&gt;</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="0194bb86a6ef494a8fd9af16c4f50d72"><span data-offset-key="0194bb86a6ef494a8fd9af16c4f50d72:0">\*\*</span><span data-offset-key="0194bb86a6ef494a8fd9af16c4f50d72:1">`>>>** pow(38, -1, mod=97) 23 **>>>** 23 * 38 % 97 == 1 True`</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c"><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:0">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:1"> For </span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:2">`[int](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#int>)`</span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:3"> operands, the three-argument form of </span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:4">`pow`</span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:5"> now allows the second argument to be negative, permitting computation of modular inverses. </span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:6">*Changed in version 3.8:*</span><span data-offset-key="c44f3fdf99b24e288964b53569d3fc5c:7"> Allow keyword arguments. Formerly, only positional arguments were supported.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393"><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:0">**`print`**</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:1">(\*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:2">*objects*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:3">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:4">*sep=' '*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:6">*end='\\n'*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:8">*file=sys.stdout*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:10">*flush=False*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:11">)Print </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:12">*objects*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:13"> to the text stream </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:14">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:15">, separated by </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:16">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:17"> and followed by </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:18">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:19">. </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:20">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:21">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:22">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:23">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:24">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:25"> and </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:26">*flush*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:27">, if present, must be given as keyword arguments. All non-keyword arguments are converted to strings like </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:28">`[str()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/stdtypes.html#str>)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:29"> does and written to the stream, separated by </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:30">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:31"> and followed by </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:32">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:33">. Both </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:34">*sep*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:35"> and </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:36">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:37"> must be strings; they can also be </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:38">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:39">, which means to use the default values. If no </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:40">*objects*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:41"> are given, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:42">`[print()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#print>)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:43"> will just write </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:44">*end*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:45">. The </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:46">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:47"> argument must be an object with a </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:48">`write(string)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:49"> method; if it is not present or </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:50">`None`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:51">, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:52">`[sys.stdout](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/sys.html#sys.stdout>)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:53"> will be used. Since printed arguments are converted to text strings, </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:54">`[print()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#print>)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:55"> cannot be used with binary mode file objects. For these, use </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:56">`file.write(...)`</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:57"> instead. Whether output is buffered is usually determined by </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:58">*file*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:59">, but if the </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:60">*flush*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:61"> keyword argument is true, the stream is forcibly flushed. </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:62">*Changed in version 3.3:*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:63"> Added the </span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:64">*flush*</span><span data-offset-key="be4c84360dac42f996725555fe6d4393:65"> keyword argument.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f"><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:2">**`property`**</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:3">(</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:4">*fget=None*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:5">, </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:6">*fset=None*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:7">, </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:8">*fdel=None*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:9">, </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:10">*doc=None*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:11">)Return a property attribute. </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:12">*fget*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:13"> is a function for getting an attribute value. </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:14">*fset*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:15"> is a function for setting an attribute value. </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:16">*fdel*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:17"> is a function for deleting an attribute value. And </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:18">*doc*</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:19"> creates a docstring for the attribute. A typical use is to define a managed attribute </span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:20">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="d548e9e6f1c9413d950271b6f90f1b6f:21">:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7"><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:0">**\`class**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:2">**C**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:3">: </span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:4">**def**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:5"> </span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:6">**init**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:7">(self): self.\_x = </span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:8">**Nonedef**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:9"> getx(self): </span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:10">**return**</span><span data-offset-key="64ced142761f48c38bf2dbee08e6ecb7:11"> self.\_x</span></span></span>

    **def** setx(self, value):    self._x = value‚Äã**def** delx(self):    **del** self._x‚Äãx = property(getx, setx, delx, "I'm the 'x' property.")`

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab"><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:0">If </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:1">*c*</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:2"> is an instance of </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:3">*C*</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:5">`c.x`</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:6"> will invoke the getter, </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:7">`c.x = value`</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:8"> will invoke the setter and </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:9">`del c.x`</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:10"> the deleter. If given, </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:11">*doc*</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:12"> will be the docstring of the property attribute. Otherwise, the property will copy </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:13">*fget*</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:14">‚Äôs docstring (if it exists). This makes it possible to create read-only properties easily using </span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:15">`[property()](<https://docs.python.org/3/library/functions.html#property>)`</span><span data-offset-key="375192a8d59f43a39fcc851f92155fab:16"> as a </span></span><a href="https://docs.python.org/3/glossary.html#term-decorator" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="1f058ec5b8334a0fb777d78c7c6ad3fd"><span data-offset-key="1f058ec5b8334a0fb777d78c7c6ad3fd:0">decorator</span></span></a><span data-key="51ccef3be56f4a23a44178e1440a9f0c"><span data-offset-key="51ccef3be56f4a23a44178e1440a9f0c:0">:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede"><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:0">**\`class**</span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:2">**Parrot**</span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:3">: </span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:4">**def**</span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:5"> </span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:6">**init**</span><span data-offset-key="413336af2e914e86807a75a2de40cede:7">(self): self.\_voltage = 100000</span></span></span>

    **@propertydef** voltage(self):    *"""Get the current voltage."""***return** self._voltage`

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec"><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:0">The </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:1">`@property`</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:2"> decorator turns the </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:3">`voltage()`</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:4"> method into a ‚Äúgetter‚Äù for a read-only attribute with the same name, and it sets the docstring for </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:5">*voltage*</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:6"> to ‚ÄúGet the current voltage.‚Äù A property object has </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:7">`getter`</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:8">, </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:9">`setter`</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:10">, and </span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:11">`deleter`</span><span data-offset-key="ecc2f024aeb047d988c757e814c69cec:12"> methods usable as decorators that create a copy of the property with the corresponding accessor function set to the decorated function. This is best explained with an example:</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b"><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:0">**\`class**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:2">**C**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:3">: </span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:4">**def**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:5"> </span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:6">**init**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:7">(self): self.\_x = </span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:8">**<a href="../cdn-cgi/l/email-protection.html" class="__cf_email__">[email¬†protected]</a>**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:9"> x(self): \*"""I'm the 'x' property."""\*</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:10">**return**</span><span data-offset-key="115c7a395b8249cda5c702e9891b2e2b:11"> self.\_x</span></span></span>

    **@x**.setter**def** x(self, value):    self._x = value‚Äã**@x**.deleter**def** x(self):    **del** self._x`

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980"><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:0">This code is exactly equivalent to the first example. Be sure to give the additional functions the same name as the original property (</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:1">`x`</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:2"> in this case.) The returned property object also has the attributes </span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:3">`fget`</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:4">, </span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:5">`fset`</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:6">, and </span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:7">`fdel`</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:8"> corresponding to the constructor arguments. </span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:9">*Changed in version 3.5:*</span><span data-offset-key="16771148f6964cdc8a420ae38b434980:10"> The docstrings of property objects are now writeable.</span></span></span>

<span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="5b4a2f39a0e54984ab9e4731a01e11c4"><span data-offset-key="5b4a2f39a0e54984ab9e4731a01e11c4:0">*class*</span><span data-offset-key="5b4a2f39a0e54984ab9e4731a01e11c4:1"> </span><span data-offset-key="5b4a2f39a0e54984ab9e4731a01e11c4:2">**`range`**</span><span data-offset-key="5b4a2f39a0e54984ab9e4731a01e11c4:3">(</span><span
